The goal is better pool/bracket score picks, not gambling advice.\n\n## Required Output\n\nEvery match must include a predicted final score/result in `home:away` format, for example `1:3`. If the fixture is listed as `Team A vs Team B`, the score must be in that same order.\n\nFor knockout-stage matches, every match must also include:\n\n- `90-min score`: the score after regulation time.\n- `AET/PK outcome`: the expected after-extra-time result, or the penalty shootout result if the match is projected to reach penalties.\n- `PK likelihood`: Low, Medium, or High, with a short reason.\n- `Aggregate incl. PKs`: a separate pool/bracket-style aggregate that adds made shootout penalties to the match goals, for example `Official: 1:1 AET; PKs: 4:3; Aggregate incl. PKs: 5:4`.\n\nDo not blend penalty shootout goals into the official match score. Keep the official score and the aggregate-including-PKs score visibly separate.\n\n## Inputs\n\n- `timezone`: The user's timezone. If it is clear from context, use that timezone. If it is not clear, ask the user to clarify before scoping fixtures or saying what is today/next.\n- `date`: Today's date in the user's timezone. Once the timezone is known, use only that timezone for date, today/current/next, and report-scope decisions.\n- `round_scope`: If the user does not specify a round, choose the current round if matches are being played today; otherwise choose the next scheduled round/matchday.\n- `competition`: FIFA World Cup unless the user specifies another tournament.\n\n## Source Priority\n\n1. Official FIFA fixtures/schedule for match list and dates.\n2. Expert correct-score predictions from reputable preview or betting-analysis sources.\n3. Opta Analyst / Opta Supercomputer for match probabilities and model framing.\n4. Sportsbook consensus or odds comparison, such as Oddschecker, for market-implied expectations.\n5. Knockout-specific market signals when available: draw-after-90 odds, extra-time odds, team-to-advance odds, and win-on-penalties odds.\n6. World Football Elo Ratings for team-strength sanity checks.\n7. Confirmed starting lineups when matches are close to kickoff: FIFA match centres or official match pages first, then ESPN/FotMob/SofaScore or comparable live match centres, then official federation/team channels.\n8. One current match preview or team-news source per match when confirmed lineups are not yet available.\n\n## Workflow\n\n1. Identify the target matches.\n   - Search for today's World Cup fixtures.\n   - Confirm the user's timezone first unless it is clear from context.\n   - Convert kickoff times into the user's timezone before deciding whether a fixture belongs to today.\n   - Include cross-midnight fixtures when they fall on the user's date, even if a source lists them under the next calendar day in ET, UTC, or local venue time.\n   - Do not mix source-listed calendar dates, venue-local dates, ET, UTC, or runtime timezone into the scope after the user's timezone is selected; mention source timezones only when useful for clarity.\n   - If there are no matches today, find the next scheduled matchday or next round.\n   - Use absolute dates and name the timezone in the report.\n\n2. Collect expert scoreline anchors.\n   - Search each fixture with terms like `prediction correct score`, `expert pick`, `score prediction`, and `odds`.\n   - Prefer sources that explicitly publish a scoreline or correct-score lean.\n   - If multiple expert scorelines exist, choose the one most consistent with the market/model and note disagreement briefly.\n\n3. Collect baseline probabilities.\n   - Prefer Opta match probabilities when available.\n   - If Opta is missing, use odds-implied probability as the baseline and say so.\n\n4. Cross-check the betting market.\n   - Compare the scoreline/winner pick with sportsbook consensus.\n   - Flag any mismatch where the expert pick and market disagree.\n\n5. For knockout-stage matches, assess extra-time and penalty risk.\n   - Use draw-after-90 probability as the main signal for whether the match can reach extra time.\n   - Use team-to-advance, win-on-penalties, and draw/under market context when available to estimate shootout likelihood.\n   - Treat closely matched teams, low totals, defensive styles, and conservative tactical incentives as higher PK-risk factors.\n   - Treat a clear favorite with strong regulation-win support as lower PK risk even if the under is popular.\n   - If explicit PK markets are missing, say the PK assessment is inferred from draw-after-90, total-goals, model, and team-strength signals.\n\n6. Sanity-check team strength.\n   - Use World Football Elo or comparable ratings.\n   - Note if a famous team appears weaker/stronger than reputation suggests.\n\n7. Add current-context checks.\n   - Look for injuries, likely rotation, suspensions, weather/travel, and motivation.\n   - For fixtures within 90 minutes of kickoff, explicitly search for confirmed starting lineups.\n   - If confirmed lineups are available, use them in the pick and state the material impact, even if the impact is \"no change.\"\n   - If confirmed lineups are unavailable, say lineups are pending only when the unresolved starter, formation, or availability question materially affects the scoreline or confidence.\n   - For fixtures more than 90 minutes away, use injuries and projected lineups normally, but avoid blanket \"wait for lineups\" language unless there is a concrete unresolved starter or tactical role.\n   - Keep this short and avoid overfitting to narrative.\n\n8. Make the scoreline pick.\n   - For each match provide: exact score, confidence, expert/model basis, and risk note.\n   - Confidence levels: High, Medium, Low.\n   - In group stages, be conservative and respect draws.\n   - In knockout stages, distinguish the regulation pick from the advancement pick.\n   - If the match is picked to go to penalties, provide the official AET score, projected PK shootout score, advancing team, and aggregate including PKs.\n   - If the match is not picked to go to penalties, still include a PK likelihood line and whether the aggregate including PKs is unchanged.\n   - Common conservative patterns: favorite `2:0` or `2:1`, close favorite `1:0`, draw-risk game `1:1`, heavy favorite `3:0` only when market/model strongly support it.\n\n9. End with an action summary.\n   - Best scoreline picks.\n   - Highest PK-risk matches.\n   - Traps/upsets to avoid.\n   - Lineup status: confirmed lineups incorporated, or specific material lineup questions still pending.\n\n## Report Format\n\nKeep Discord output concise. Avoid markdown tables. Use markdown headings to make the report scannable: `##` for report sections and `###` for each game pick. In `Scoreline Picks`, write each game as a short paragraph entry with the pick in the heading. Put `Basis:` and `Risk:` on their own lines below the pick.\n\nRecommended structure:\n\n- Scope line: `Report scope: [round/matchday], [absolute date range]`\n- Timezone-aware scope example: `Report scope: [round/matchday], Saturday, June 27, 2026 in U.S. Pacific time`\n- `## Scoreline Picks`\n  `### Team A vs Team B: 2:1 - Confidence: Medium`\n  `Basis: expert pick/model/market summary`\n  `Risk: ...`\n- Knockout-stage heading example without PKs:\n  `### Team A vs Team B: 2:1 - Aggregate incl. PKs: 2:1 - Confidence: Medium`\n  `90-min score: Team A 2:1 Team B`\n  `AET/PK outcome: Team A advances in regulation; no PK aggregate adjustment`\n  `PK likelihood: Low - market/model favor a regulation winner`\n  `Basis: expert pick/model/market summary`\n  `Risk: ...`\n- Knockout-stage heading example with PKs:\n  `### Team A vs Team B: 1:1 AET, Team A advance 4:3 on PKs - Aggregate incl. PKs: 5:4 - Confidence: Low`\n  `90-min score: Team A 1:1 Team B`\n  `AET/PK outcome: 1:1 AET; Team A win PKs 4:3`\n  `PK likelihood: High - draw-after-90 and low-total signals are elevated`\n  `Basis: expert pick/model/market summary`\n  `Risk: ...`\n- `## Best Scoreline Leans`\n- `## Highest PK-Risk Matches` for knockout-stage reports\n- `## Traps / Upsets To Avoid`\n- `## Lineup Status`\n- `## Sources`\n\nLineup status examples:\n\n- Confirmed: `Lineups checked: Norway start Haaland, Odegaard, and Sorloth; no change to 2:1 Norway.`\n- Pending: `Lineups pending: wait on Mexico striker/keeper because it affects 1:1 vs 2:1.`\n\n## Guardrails\n\n- Always browse/search current sources before making picks.\n- Include links to sources used.\n- Do not present scorelines as guaranteed outcomes.\n- Do not encourage wagering or bankroll decisions unless explicitly asked; even then, keep it informational.\n- If expert scoreline data is thin or conflicting, say so and lower confidence.\n- Do not tell the user to wait for final lineups when confirmed lineups have already been found. Prediction</strong></h2>\n817-\n818-\n819-\n820:<p>Despite their injury concerns at the back and inconsistent attacking displays in North America, England are comfortable favourites for the meeting with DR Congo.</p>\n821-\n822-\n823-\n824:<p>The Opta supercomputer&#8217;s 25,000 pre-match simulations saw them come out on top 73.9% of the time after 90 minutes, while DR Congo were only victorious in 11.3% of the projections.</p>\n825-\n826-\n827-\n828:<p>The likelihood of a draw after 90 minutes sits at 14.8%, and with this World Cup having an extra knockout round both sides will be keen to avoid extra time in the last 32.</p>\n829-\n830-\n--\n834-\n835-\n836:<figure id=\"figure-250252\"class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img decoding=\"async\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" But it’s their centre-forward, <a href=\"https://theanalyst.com/players/3195/folarin-balogun\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-analyst-id=\"3195\" data-thumbnail-url=\"https://theanalyst.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/default-player-50x50.jpeg\" style=\"--ta-person-link-thumb: url('https://theanalyst.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/default-player-50x50.jpeg')\" class=\"ta-person-link\">Folarin Balogun</a>, who has made the biggest impression so far.</p>\n698-\n699-\n--\n703-\n704-\n705:<p>A well-rested squad, Pulisic’s return, and Balogun’s form all combine to make USA particularly well-set to prosper against Bosnia &#8211; but history is not on their side. They have lost seven of their eight World Cup knockout-stage matches, conceding 22 goals. Their one win came against Mexico in the 2002 round of 16, winning 2-0 with goals from Brian McBride and Donovan.</p>\n706-\n707-\n708-\n709:<p>Still, they would not trade their experience for Bosnia’s lack thereof. This is Bosnia’s first-ever appearance at the World Cup knockout stages, and they weren’t entirely convincing during the group stage of this tournament, despite their progression.</p>\n710-\n711-\n--\n715-\n716-\n717:<figure id=\"figure-250317\"class=\"wp-block-image aligncenter size-large\"><img decoding=\"async\" width=\"1024\" height=\"576\" src=\"https://theanalyst.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/06/bosnia-v-qatar-xg-race-1024x576.jpeg\" alt=\"Bosnia v Qatar xG race\" class=\"wp-image-250317\" srcset=\"https://theanalyst.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/06/bosnia-v-qatar-xg-race-1024x576.jpeg 1024w, https://theanalyst.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/06/bosnia-v-qatar-xg-race-300x169.jpeg 300w, https://theanalyst.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/06/bosnia-v-qatar-xg-race-768x432.jpeg 768w, https://theanalyst.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/06/bosnia-v-qatar-xg-race-1536x864.jpeg 1536w, https://theanalyst.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/06/bosnia-v-qatar-xg-race-2048x1152.jpeg 2048w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure>\n718-\n719-\n--\n723-\n724-\n725:<p>One of Bosnia’s main weapons is their physicality. They have the tallest squad at the tournament, with an average height of 6-foot-1, and they have made the most of that advantage, scoring three goals from corners. The last team to score more at a single edition was England in 2018, with four.</p>\n726-\n727-\n--\n731-\n732-\n733:<p>Attention should also be paid to the intriguing story of Bosnia winger <a href=\"https://theanalyst.com/players/8159/esmir-bajraktarevic\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-analyst-id=\"8159\" data-thumbnail-url=\"https://theanalyst.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/default-player-50x50.jpeg\" style=\"--ta-person-link-thumb: url('https://theanalyst.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/default-player-50x50.jpeg')\" class=\"ta-person-link\">Esmir Bajraktarevic</a>, who was in fact born in the United States in 2004, where his family eventually emigrated after fleeing the Bosnian War. Bajraktarević decided to represent his parents’ nation of birth despite receiving his first international cap for USA in a 2024 friendly against Slovenia, switching allegiances a few months later.</p>\n734-\n735-\n736-\n737:<h2 class=\"wp-block-heading has-text-align-center\"><strong><strong>USA vs Bosnia-Herzegovina Head-to-Head</strong></strong></h2>\n738-\n739-\n740-\n741:<p>This will be the fourth meeting between USA and Bosnia and Herzegovina, with the Stars and Stripes unbeaten in the first three (W2 D1), all in friendlies from 2013 to 2021.</p>\n742-\n743-\n--\n747-\n748-\n749:<h2 class=\"wp-block-heading has-text-align-center\"><strong><strong>USA vs Bosnia-Herzegovina href=\"https://google.com/preferences/source?q=lastwordonsports.com\"\n--\n709-\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<header class=\"entry-header mb-6\">\n710-\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h1 class=\"entry-title text-3xl md:text-4xl font-bold text-gray-900 leading-tight\">\n711:\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t2026 World Cup Round of 32 Predictions Including England vs DR Congo\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</h1>\n712-\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</header>\n713-\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n714-\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-content content-styled max-w-none\">\n715:\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>On Wednesday at the World Cup, we&#8217;ll see one of the tournament favorites, England, taking on underdogs DR Congo in Atlanta. The hosts USA take on Bosnia, and the Senegal vs Belgium clash is a match of two teams that have yet to fulfill their expectations this tournament. As always, we preview and predict every match.</p>\n716:<h2>England vs DR Congo (Wednesday July 1st in Atlanta)</h2>\n717:<p>There&#8217;s a degree fear and loathing for England when they take on DR Congo in the first knockout stage hurdle on Wednesday, indoors in Atlanta. DR Congo have put together a great tournament, a narrow defeat against Colombia their only negative result, as they <a href=\"https://theseyereport.substack.com/p/dr-congo-stifled-portugal-and-left\" target=\"_blank\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">stifled Portugal into a draw</a> and then came back to comprehensively defeat Uzbekistan to secure a last 32 place.</p>\n718-<div class=\"lwos-incontent-ad\" style=\"margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; clear: both;\"><div id=\"snack-incontent-1\"></div></div>\n719-\n720:<p>England beat Croatia in a thrilling opening match 4-2, the momentum was real, and then it stalled in a big way, as they were held to an extremely dull draw against Ghana, unable to score, unable to unlock the Black Stars low block. Matchday 3 saw victory against Panama, fueled by Jude Bellingham&#8217;s great second half, as Panama hung around and kept it competitive before eventually becoming overwhelmed.</p>\n721:<p>England are the far more talented team here, they will sit on the ball, they will have the vast majority of the chances, but DR Congo are capable at counterattacking and are willing to defend all day if that&#8217;s what it takes to pull off this significant upset.</p>\n722-<div class=\"lwos-incontent-ad\" style=\"margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; clear: both;\"><div id=\"snack-incontent-2\"></div></div>\n723-\n724:<p>The squad choices for England will matter significantly. Harry Kane remains their most important goal scorer but at times he&#8217;s been dropping back and hasn&#8217;t been able to get involved effectively. Jude Bellingham has been England&#8217;s best player, carrying the #10 role, but he&#8217;s often been without support, players like Bukayo Saka and Anthony Gordon have been ineffective at creating and breaking teams down. Tuchel tried Morgan Rogers and Rogers was invisible in the time he played. There are injury concerns around Reece James, who is unlikely to feature, and Jarell Quansah, this is a team missing Trent Alexander-Arnold in the squad right now.</p>\n725:<p>You can&#8217;t fault the England defence, they have kept two clean sheets against teams that are likely to setup similar to DR Congo. This should be an England win as DR Congo with Yoane Wissa simply don&#8217;t create a ton of chances, but it&#8217;s not going to be without toil, someone has to step up and help Bellingham, and Tuchel should consider the bold move of playing two strikers, getting minutes for either Ollie Watkins or <a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/football/2026/jun/26/world-cup-england-toney-on-good-terms-with-tuchel-and-awaiting-his-chance\" target=\"_blank\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Ivan Toney,</a> so Kane can play his ideal game.</p>\n726:<p>Prediction: <strong>England</strong> 1-0</p>\n727-<h3>Belgium vs Senegal (Wednesday July 1st in Seattle)</h3>\n728-<p class=\"\" style=\"max-width: 1280px\"><smartframe-embed class=\"smartframe_wp_element\" customer-id=\"b0c95bc04383cef69c6b47df872135cf\" image-id=\"WmOBZ2B9OWpb\" style=\"width: 100%; display: inline-flex; max-width: 6819px; aspect-ratio: 6819/3836;\" ></smartframe-embed></p>\n--\n732-<p>Leandro Trossard has been their player of the tournament, the Arsenal player is key to whatever Belgium could do in this tournament, as Jeremy Doku, Kevin De Bruyne, and Youri Tielmans playing together has resulted in too much overlap at times. De Bruyne was expected to be the talisman, but he tries too hard trying to force plays sometimes and things crumble for the Red Devils.</p>\n733-<p>In the back, Belgium inspires more confidence, Thibaut Courtois is still world class and gives them a real advantage.</p>\n734:<p>Belgium will be underdogs if we see the version of Senegal that went out and got a 5-0 result to secure qualification against Iraq on matchday 3. Senegal looked much improved, after losses to great France and Norway teams where they were defensively disorganized. Veteran defensive leader Kalidou <a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/football/2026/jun/25/senegals-world-cup-is-hanging-by-a-thread-after-comedy-of-errors-on-and-off-pitch\" target=\"_blank\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Koulibaly</a> has been out of form and shambolic, and their star captain Sadio Mane is also starting to show his age. Belgium can score, Crystal Palace&#8217;s Ismaila Sarr has three goals this tournament. This should be an open and free flowing game, both teams will want to get after it. Edouard Mendy hasn&#8217;t been great in goal for Senegal, and now he&#8217;s <a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/AfricaSoccerZone/posts/-update-%C3%A9douard-mendys-injury-situationsenegal-goalkeeper-%C3%A9douard-mendy-has-temp/993424179984904/\" target=\"_blank\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">injured</a>, that lets Yehvann Diouf put on the goalkeeping gloves.</p>\n735-<div class=\"lwos-incontent-ad\" style=\"margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; clear: both;\"><div id=\"snack-incontent-repeater-1\"></div></div>\n736-\n737:<p>Senegal don&#8217;t have a good matchup here unless they can figure it out defensively. Belgium struggles to unlock a low block, but should be able to defend enough to limit Senegal&#8217;s scoring. It&#8217;s quite possible this game goes to extra time or even penalties.</p>\n738:<p>Prediction: <strong>Belgium</strong> 3-2 (after extra time)</p>\n739-<h3>USA vs Bosnia (Wednesday July 1st in San Francisco)</h3>\n740-<p class=\"\" style=\"max-width: 1280px\"><smartframe-embed class=\"smartframe_wp_element\" customer-id=\"b0c95bc04383cef69c6b47df872135cf\" image-id=\"WmOBBy6oNfgn\" style=\"width: 100%; display: inline-flex; max-width: 5375px; aspect-ratio: 5375/3584;\" ></smartframe-embed></p>\n--\n744-<p>Team USA with their first-choice XI <a href=\"https://lastwordonsports.com/football/2026/06/20/with-flair-and-consistency-the-2026-world-cup-host-nations-usa-mexico-and-canada-reach-the-world-cup-knockout-phase/\" target=\"_blank\" target=\"_self\">hammered</a> Paraguay in the opener, before keeping a clean sheet and comfortably defeating a good Australia side. Against Turkiye it was a 3-2 defeat, but without their starters, the defence leaked too many goals.</p>\n745-<p>Mauricio Pochettino&#8217;s USA has more firepower, if fit, Christian <a href=\"https://www.espn.com/soccer/story/_/id/49179061/pulisic-starts-bench-united-states-turner-goal\" target=\"_blank\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Pulisic</a> leads the attack and can feed Folarin Balogun all game. Matt Freese has proven to be capable in goal, and at 38-years-old Tim Ream is an underrated defender. The US will get at this game, and Bosnia doesn&#8217;t strike enough defensive confidence to win in all likelihood, but nerves could be a factor for the hosts.</p>\n746:<p>Prediction: <strong>United States</strong> 2-1</p>\n747-<p>Main Photo Credit: Smartframe Images</p>\n748-\n--\n767-\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2\">\n768-\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span season, collecting 33 points across 19 top-flight outings, with only league winners Liverpool (38) and second-placed Arsenal (35) earning more points on the road.</p><p>With a later start date of competitive action this term compared to Saturday's hosts, Forest are only just commencing their pre-season plans, with matches against the likes of Estoril, Birmingham City and Fiorentina booked in before a top-flight opener with Brentford on August 17.</p><p>The Tricky Trees have made a slow start to the summer transfer window, although the arrival of Igor Jesus from Brazilian giants Botafogo
